---
sidebar_label: Amazon Web Services
---

# AWS Resource Data Models

:::info

See [How to Collect AWS Resource Data](../../how-to-guides/data-sources/collect-aws-resource-data.mdx) for step-by-step directions to configure Fix Inventory to collect [Amazon Web Services (AWS)](https://aws.amazon.com) resources.

:::
